msg:Here is a concise, positive review for an overnight stay at the Na Lotus Hotel, A Luxury Collection Hotel in Nanning:

Luxurious Overnight at the Na Lotus Hotel

I had the pleasure of staying at the Na Lotus Hotel, A Luxury Collection Hotel during my recent visit to Nanning, and it exceeded all of my expectations. From the moment I stepped into the grand lobby, I was struck by the hotel's elegant, modern design and attentive staff. My room was spacious and beautifully appointed, with high-end furnishings, a large comfortable bed, and stunning views of the city skyline. The hotel's amenities, including the expansive fitness center and serene spa, allowed me to fully relax and unwind. The on-site dining options were also superb, with creative dishes showcasing local Guangxi cuisine. Overall, my stay at the Na Lotus Hotel was a true luxury experience, and I would highly recommend it to anyone seeking an exceptional overnight in Nanning.

I have to say that the view from the high floor is beautiful. The room is very spacious and bright, and the overall color tone is light and fresh; the facilities are complete, the bedding is also comfortable, and functional pillows can be provided as an extra, and disposable slippers are a plus, which makes it feel especially comfortableüòå
The breakfast variety is rich, covering almost all the specialties of Guangxi, sour food, various noodles, and the eggs in their restaurant are the most cooked in the restaurant I have ever seen, which can be called an egg feast!
The staff service is also pretty good, enthusiastic and meticulous, in line with the standards of high-end hotels.

msg:The location is convenient. When you arrive at the lobby on the first floor, the waiter will take the initiative to help you take your luggage, change the luggage tag, and deliver it directly to the room.
The hotel lobby is on the highest floor, 80 floors. Check-in is done in a seated manner. It is not affected by the May Day holiday. The process is orderly and efficient. It can be seen that the management is in place, which adds points to the first impression.
Breakfast is on the 79th floor, with a wide view and rich dishes. The taste of Guangxi specialty noodles such as Laoyoufen and Luoshifen is not bad. There is a small children's play area at the entrance. My brother is over 120cm, but the front desk still considerately waived the meal fee. Thank you!
The constant temperature swimming pool is especially good at night. You need to bring your own swimsuit, swimming cap and swimming ring. There is a sauna room. I praise the hotel pool caretaker, who is very serious and responsible. There is no need to worry about the safety hazards of children swimming.
The hotel lobby can rent national costumes for free shooting. You need to pay a deposit of 2,000 and return it on the same day. Children are very cute in them, but it‚Äôs a pity that they don‚Äôt match the style of the hotel. There is no shooting area for the scene. It is recommended to build one.
Due to the flight delay, we delayed check-out by 3 o'clock. The service is really remarkable. If you come to Nanning, I highly recommend staying here.

name:s‚Äça‚Äçb‚Äçr‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äça‚Äç0‚Äç3‚Äç1‚Äç3
info:Superior City-view King
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Solo travelers
info:7 Reviews
rating:4.8
posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:üåπThis time I stayed in Nanning for only 20 hours. Choosing a hotel is still my favorite and most entangled part of every trip. I was wavering between "Shangri-La" and "Luxury Collection". In the end, I chose The Luxury Collection, the first luxury hotel series to enter Nanning before Shangri-La.

üåπ"Luxury Collection" is not well known in China. I personally think it may be related to the pure Chinese translation: "Luxury Collection", which literally feels like a mediocre business collection hotel. In fact, "Luxury Collection" is a luxury brand under Marriott with the same level as Ritz and St. Regis. There are currently five hotels in China.

üåπEach hotel in The Luxury Collection has its own unique theme. The theme of this one in Nanning is "Lotus". In the Longguang Century Building of Longguang Group, the business gene is definitely there. What is noteworthy is the 360-degree and 180-degree high-altitude city view of the hotel's public areas and rooms, and the close view of Qingxiu Mountain (the only 5A scenic spot in Nanning). This kind of landscape is unique not only in Nanning, but also in hotels around the world. "Good view" seems to be the label of "Luxury Collection".

üåπ"Nanning Longguang Nalian Luxury Collection Hotel" is designed by the world-renowned design company HBA, and the design inspiration comes from the folk legend story "Yuemei Hanging the Moon" in Zhuangxiang. HBA was founded in 1965 and is the first company on earth to be established with hotels as a dedicated design project. It is one of the first international design companies to enter China after the reform and opening up. It is the design responsible for many well-known hotels in China. It is the project designer of the familiar Guangzhou White Swan Hotel in 1983.

üåπThe hotel's fragrance supplies come from the Swedish niche brand Byredo, which is fragrant but not greasy. The bedding comes from the Italian luxury textile product Frette. The fabric is solid, and the stiff and soft knitting density allows the body and skin to truly feel the proper support, making rest and sleep safe and refreshing.

üåπThe hotel opened in 2019, with 290 guest rooms on 13 floors, and the basic room type is also 49-5*** meters, which is enough. The lobby is on the 80th floor. When you get to the 80th floor, the Chinese restaurant is on the left when you get out of the elevator. On the other side is the Yunxiao Lounge in the lobby bar (there are bands on Thursdays, Fridays and Saturdays); the Nalian Restaurant on the 79th floor is also a breakfast location. You can eat Guilin rice noodles for breakfast, which can be mixed or soup. There are two types of soups: snail noodles and Laoyou noodles (spicy and sour); the 77th floor is a gym, sky pool, and SPA; 290 rooms are distributed on floors 63-75.

üåπThe cloud city skyline of the hotel swimming pool reminds people of the Shard in London and the Luxury Collection of Prince Gallery Kioicho in Tokyo... The height and view of the lobby remind people of the St. Regis in Shenzhen... The Luxury Collection in Dubai costs more than 10,000, Kyoto costs 9K+, Tokyo costs 6K+, Seoul costs 3K+, and the most powerful one in Seychelles costs about 10,000 US dollars a night, but what? This one in Nanning costs ¬•900 per room per night, including breakfast, what else do you want?
